"Aɣurru d yiwen waggas gar waggasen i izemren ad ihudd tudert n umdan neɣ i izemren ad t-yesnegren wakali. War amiji, d aɣurru i d-yettaǧǧan ccwami lqayen. Drus-itent tzemmar i uzuɣer n uxeddaɛ ɣer tegnit n ṣṣwav. Tesseggray-d s calwaw ɣef wallen, ɣevvu n teflest, tiɣersiwt n wassaɣ, tamḍelt n tirga d yisenfaṛen yeţwaṣkan "deg sin/gar sin". Nnig n unnect-a, taẓẓayt n uɣurru tzeddel ɣef yiman, i aɣ-yettaǧǧan nḥekkem s zzuṛ ɣef yiman-nneɣ seg tugti n tuzzma, anuɣni, reffu... i izemren ad d-iglun s temrart i yiri," i d-yura Ali Belhot.

Muḥend Belqasem: "Dda AmarM, d amdan ur zmireɣ ad ak-d-weṣfeɣ, ayen i d-nniɣ fell-as drus. D aselmad meqqren i ḥemmlen yinelmaden deg tesdawit, d ameɛnas n tsertit seg zik, d asadur n tarwa n Bennai Weɛli, .... d amɣar yelmed taqbaylit s zreb. Deg Tatoeba, d netta i d-yessuqulen ugar seg teglizit ɣer teqbaylit neɣ seg teqbaylit ɣer teglizit. Aḥuddu aḥunnu ɣef yimeɣnasen." Dda AmarM i Muḥend: " "Tanemmirt-ik, a Muḥend. Lemmer mačči d widak am kečč iyi-d-ifkan tabɣest i tira deg Tatoeba, seld Tarik Tinouche iyi-d-innan «Aru, ma ad taruḍ, war tugdi !», tili ur ţawḍeɣ ara armi ţxiḍiɣ taqbaylit s tuqqna n wallen. Zik, ţxemmimeɣ ayen ţaruɣ s tṛumit, tura swingimeɣ srid s teqbaylit seld ad aruɣ ye-s. Ayɣer? Acku, d tutlayt-iw tayemmaţ. Wagi yakk, s tejmilt-nwen akken ma tellam! Anef tura i tutlayin-nniḍen am tneglizit i sseqdaceɣ akken aɣ-d-ḍefṛen wiyaḍ: tura ha-ten imarikanen ţgallan kan s yinzan n teqbaylit i d-sseɣtiɣ ar tneglizit, talmanit, tarusit, atg. D asbucceɛ n udlis aqbayli. Akka i walaɣ iswi n tira d-yessalayen iseɣ."

Walaɣ, llina hah, yiwen u Berṭeẓẓ, degmi yennuɣna yewwet-as kra n ukelluẓ akken n ccemma. Nniɣ-as, wagi tura, seg widak yesnegren ṭṭaba, u mazal! Iɛreq-as ugafa Dɣa yuɣal yeţfa. Tfukk-iyi cemma di Kanada qrib i hebleɣ. Ḍaqeɣ ad d-awḍeɣ ɣer usafag. Ma temmugreḍ-t-id deg uvrid yeqlev ucenfir-is seg uqelluẓ-nni i s-yerra, ak-d-yeţvin iteddu-d yeţfay. Yeţnudum ɣef yiman-is. Ṣekren ikeṛwuza-is.

"Aɣurru d yiwen waggas gar waggasen i izemren ad ihudd tudert n umdan neɣ i izemren ad t-yesnegren wakali. War amiji, d aɣurru i d-yettaǧǧan ccwami lqayen. Drus-itent tzemmar i uzuɣer n uxeddaɛ ɣer tegnit n ṣṣwav. Tesseggray-d s calwaw ɣef wallen, ɣebbu n teflest, tiɣersiwt n wassaɣ, tamḍelt n tirga d yisenfaṛen yettwaṣkan "deg sin/gar sin". Nnig wannect-a, taẓẓayt n uɣurru tzeddel ɣef yiman, i aɣ-yettaǧǧan nḥekkem s zzuṛ ɣef yiman-nneɣ seg tugti n tuzzma, anuɣni, reffu... i izemren ad d-iglun s temrart i yiri", i d-yura gma-t-neɣ Ali Belhot.
Aɣurru d yiwen waggas gar waggasen i izemren ad ihudd tudert n umdan neɣ i izemren ad t-yesnegren wakali." i d-yura gma-t-neɣ Ali Belhot.

D amaynut yessefṛaḥen: Ass-a tutlayt Taqbaylit tewweḍ ar weswir wis 9 n tutlayin timezwura deg n Tatoeba. Tatoeba yesɛa 388 n tutlayin anda tella Teqbaylit deg umḍiq wis 9. Tiririt i widak yeqqaren “ acuɣeṛ d ‘Taqbayli’ mačči d ‘Tamaziɣt’ ? ”
D amaynut yessefṛaḥen: Ass-a tutlayt Taqbaylit tewweḍ ar weswir wis 9 n tutlayin timezwura deg n Tatoeba.
Tatoeba yesɛa 388 n tutlayin anda tella Teqbaylit deg umḍiq wis 9. Tiririt i widak yeqqaren “ acuɣeṛ d ‘Taqbayli’ mačči d ‘Tamaziɣt’ ? ”
Tatoeba yesɛa 388 n tutlayin anda tella Teqbaylit deg umḍiq wis 9.
Tiririt i widak yeqqaren “ acuɣeṛ d ‘Taqbayli’ mačči d ‘Tamaziɣt’ ? ”
Tamezwarut: S wudem n tussna: tamaziɣt d tawacult n tatlayin (une famille de langues), mačči d tagruma n tantaliwin (ensemble de dialectes). Tis-snat: Widak yebɣan ad ɣṛen ɣef temsalt-a ad walin ukessar imagraden n Koosmann (2012), Bendjaballah & Ben Si Said (2015), Chaker (2016: 4-6) akked Frajzyngier (2018).
Tamezwarut: S wudem n tussna: tamaziɣt d tawacult n tatlayin (une famille de langues), mačči d tagruma n tantaliwin (ensemble de dialectes).
Tis-snat: Widak yebɣan ad ɣṛen ɣef temsalt-a ad walin ukessar imagraden n Koosmann (2012), Bendjaballah & Ben Si Said (2015), Chaker (2016: 4-6) akked Frajzyngier (2018). Akka i d-yura umḍebber n terbaεt taqbaylit deg Tatoeba.
Tis-snat: Widak yebɣan ad ɣṛen ɣef temsalt-a ad walin ukessar imagraden n Koosmann (2012), Bendjaballah & Ben Si Said (2015), Chaker (2016: 4-6) akked Frajzyngier (2018).
Akka i d-yura umḍebber n terbaεt taqbaylit deg Tatoeba.
Amek i nezmer ad naweḍ ar yiswi-nneɣ ? 1. Iqbayliyen akk yessnen ad arun zemren ad ttekkin deg leqdic ɣef teqbaylit (widak yebɣan ad ttekkin, ad kecmen ar Tatoeba.org). 2. Widak yellan yakkan qeddcen deg Tatoeba, yelha ma nefka-yas kra n ddhis ussan-a akken ad nili ger 10 n tutlayin timezwura deg ussan i d-iteddun.
Amek i nezmer ad naweḍ ar yiswi-nneɣ ?
"1. Iqbayliyen akk yessnen ad arun zemren ad ttekkin deg leqdic ɣef teqbaylit (widak yebɣan ad ttekkin, ad kecmen ar Tatoeba.org). 2. Widak yellan yakkan qeddcen deg Tatoeba, yelha ma nefka-yas kra n ddhis ussan-a akken ad nili ger 10 n tutlayin timezwura deg ussan i d-iteddun", i d-yura diɣ A.Bedar, ass n 05/11/2020 deg Tatoeba s teqbaylit.
"1. Iqbayliyen akk yessnen ad arun zemren ad ttekkin deg leqdic ɣef teqbaylit (widak yebɣan ad ttekkin, ad kecmen ar Tatoeba.org), i d-yura diɣ A.Bedar, ass n 05/11/2020 deg Tatoeba s teqbaylit.
"2. Widak yellan yakkan qeddcen deg Tatoeba, yelha ma nefka-yas kra n ddhis ussan-a akken ad nili ger 10 n tutlayin timezwura deg ussan i d-iteddun", i d-yura diɣ A.Bedar, ass n 05/11/2020 deg Tatoeba s teqbaylit.
« Taqbaylit d arraw-is kan ara tt-irefden. Tanemmirt tameqqṛant i widak iqeddcen ussan-a s waṭas deg Tatoeba. Bɣiɣ ad d-fkeɣ kra n yismawen n yemdanen iwumi ara nini ‘tanemmirt tameqqṛant’, meɛna ma yella win i ttuɣ ad iyi-isemmeḥ: Muḥend Belqasem Aqemmud, Igider Budo d Massa Tigidert, Slimane Selyan Amiri , Imal Aqvayli (tamacint n usdegdeg), Yazid Iflis (Tamacint n usdegdeg tis 2), Samir Tighzert , Malek Houd , Dda Amar Mecheri , Kahina Messaoudi , Farid At Musa , Rafik Haddadene , Hacene Hocine Kacete , d nekki Amazigh Bedar ... Ma yella win i nettu ad ɣ-isemmeḥ. Aṭas nnayeḍ ur d-bdireɣ ara ismawen-nsen, meɛna leqdic-nsen yesɛa azal meqqṛen, ulac win ara ten-ittun. Taqbaylit d arraw-is kan ara tt-irefden », i d-yura diɣ A.Bedar, ass n 05/11/2020 deg Tatoeba s teqbaylit.

Akki!
Assa n 8 di Meɣres, am akka d tafaska n tmeṭṭut. Ta d jida-t-neɣ, ta d tayemmaţ, ta d weltma-t-neɣ, ta d yelli-t-neɣ, ta ɛad d tin wukud neţţemɛntay deg tmeddurt, ha nemṣada, ha nemgarad.
Asḥissef yellan, ɣef tid i iɛemmden ad qqiment yess-nsent deg miḥṛas neɣ ţmekkinent arraw-nsent ar tefrut. Wamma tid, aḥlil, yenneɛtaben, yeţţuḥegfen, yelluẓen, yeţwaten, yeţwanɣan, yeţwagezmen d tiftatin i wuccanen, d acu ara d-nini fell-asent, ma mačči d awal uṛzin?
Tid ur neẓri anda ţmeḍwayent, tid yesmenyifen aɛluḍ d uqajmar, yerna d illel i yellan gar-asen, tid ur neẓri ula d argaz ur nḥemmel tid wukud yenḥaf, ilaq ad ẓrent ula d neţţa ixuṣs-as wezgen.
Tilmeẓyin-nneɣ d yilmeẓyen yeţwarzen, tid akked wid yeţnadin kan tayeţ ɣer win d tin ur-ţ-nesɛi, gar iɣallen n umwanes d temwanest kan yellan deg ssɛaya n wid i umi teţţunefk tegniţ i ifuṛsen wid ten-yeṛban deg miḥyaf n tumert, i sḍemɛen s yilellucen, s tirga, wigi ilaq-asen ad kerrcen aqendur akken ad nadin ɣef tmeddurt ara ten-yessufɣen seg tillas d timḍellas, s yiman-nsen, ama d tallest ama d alles.
Yir zwaǧ tif-it tlelli deg tiɣɣubna d leḥṛis, imi igli d win wuɣur neţţazzal s wudem ara ɣ-igen tirigliwin d tigejda n usirem.
M'ur nfaq, m'ur faqent tura, ha-ţ-an timetti-nsent d tin-nneɣ, tameddurt-nneɣ irkulli, segmi i ţ-iɣunza, yefka-ţ weqjun i yiffis.
Ulac win umi nḥettem ad d-isseɣli igenni.
Werǧin neggul i useɣli n yigenni.

Yeččur uyeddid!

Yella win i k-innan seɣli-d igenni?
Ur ţalaseɣ awal-iw, imi n tzemmurt!
Abazin, ula ay tyifen i usizdeg n ufwad. Awal-agi, ad s-d-afeɣ anida ara t-sneṭḍeɣ.
